        var flyTAPModule = angular.module('flyTAPModule', ["angucomplete-alt"]);
        flyTAPModule.run(function ($rootScope) {
            $rootScope.marketCode = "ar";
            $rootScope.languageCode = "es-ES";
            $rootScope.mode = "display";
            $rootScope.menuId = "{D147B706-83B1-4247-B862-E2539A090D93}";
            $rootScope.translation = {};
            $rootScope.translation.victoriaMiles = "Millas";
            $rootScope.configuration = {};
            $rootScope.configuration.invalidEmail = "Introducir e-mail v&#225;lido";
            $rootScope.configuration.invalidPin = "Introducir PIN v&#225;lido";
            $rootScope.configuration.profileLink = "";
        });
        var initHeaderStatic = function () {

            siteLoaded();
            pagePostInitialization();
            initializeAcessibility();
            initializeHeader();
            initializeQuickLogin("?sc_mark=AR&amp;sc_lang=es-ES", "Introducir e-mail válido", "Introducir PIN válido");
            initializeIntent();
        }
        document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function () {
            initLocale("es-ES");
            pageStartUp();
            templateModifier();
        });
        window.onload = function () {
        };
        document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function () {

            /*
            * Function called to hide the notifications presented in the
            * top notification menu near quick-login
            */
            $(document).on('click', 'a.js-handleHeaderNotification, button.js-handleHeaderNotification', function (e) {

                var NotificationID = $(this).parents("li").attr('id');
                var redirectURL = $(this).attr("href");
                var status = "";
                if ($(this).hasClass('js-Accept')) {
                    UpdateNotificationStatus(NotificationID, "ReadAccepted", "", redirectURL, '?sc_mark=AR&amp;sc_lang=es-ES');
                    status = "ReadAccepted";
                } else {
                    UpdateNotificationStatus(NotificationID, "ReadDismissed", "", redirectURL, '?sc_mark=AR&amp;sc_lang=es-ES');
                    status = "ReadDismissed";
                }

                $("#" + NotificationID).children(".js-notifications-wrapper").addClass("is-inactive");
                $("#" + NotificationID).find('.wrapper-button').hide();

                var formattedID = GetNotificationFormatedID(NotificationID);
                if (!$("#" + formattedID).children().hasClass("is-inactive")) {
                    UpdateNotificationsNumber();
                }

                var pageNotificationID = "#page_" + NotificationID;
                if ($(pageNotificationID).length != 0) {
                    updateNotificationPageItem(pageNotificationID, status);
                }

                return false;
            });
        });
    </script>

    <script aria-hidden="true">
            document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function () {
                var ctas = $('.ga-banner-cta');
                var index = 1;
                ctas.each(function () {
                    var sliderDiv = $(this).closest('.mod-gradient-layer.slick-slide');
                    if (!sliderDiv.hasClass('slick-cloned')) {
                        $(this).addClass('ga-bigbanner-cta-' + index.toString());
                        index = index + 1;
                    }
                });
                var masks = $('.ga-banner-cta .mask');
                masks.each(function () {
                    var sliderDiv = $(this).closest('.mod-gradient-layer.slick-slide');
                    if (!sliderDiv.hasClass('slick-cloned')) {
                        $(this).addClass('ga-cta-mask-' + index.toString());
                        index = index + 1;
                    }
                });
            });
        </script>

    var lastAdultVal = 0;
    var multiCityComercial = "https://book.flytap.com/r3air/tap/DeepLink.aspx?market=AR&language=es&searchType=multi";

    function SetBookingAutocomplete() {
        if ($('#booking-type-2').parent().hasClass('checked')) {
            $('.ibe-origin').removeClass("js-ibeairport-origin");
            $('.ibe-destination').removeClass("js-ibeairport-destination");

            $(".ibe-origin").addClass("js-ibevictoriaairport-origin");
            $(".ibe-destination").addClass("js-ibevictoriaairport-destination");
        }
        else {
            $('.ibe-origin').addClass("js-ibeairport-origin");
            $('.ibe-destination').addClass("js-ibeairport-destination");

            $(".ibe-origin").removeClass("js-ibevictoriaairport-origin");
            $(".ibe-destination").removeClass("js-ibevictoriaairport-destination");

        }

        var eraseOrigin = true;
        var eraseDestination = true;
        var originInput = $(".ibe-origin").val();
        var destinationInput = $(".ibe-destination").val();

        if (originInput != '' && originInput != null && destinationInput != '' && destinationInput != null && originInput.length >= 4) {

            var origin = originInput.substring(1, 4);
            var destination = destinationInput.substring(1, 4);

            // See if the city pair is valid in the given context (Buy with money or buy with miles)
            // If valid the inputs shouldn't be erased
            if ($('#booking-type-2').parent().hasClass('checked')) {

                var originLST = getIBEVictoriaOrigins();
                for(i = 0; i < originLST.length; i++){
                    if(originLST[i].substring(1, 4) == origin) {
                        eraseOrigin = false;
                        break;
                    }
                }

                if(!eraseOrigin && destination != '' && destination != null){
                    var destinationsLST = getDestinationForVictoria(origin);
                    for(i = 0; i < destinationsLST.length; i++){
                        if(destinationsLST[i].substring(1, 4) == destination) {
                            eraseDestination = false;
                            break;
                        }
                    }
                }
            } else {

                var originLST = getIBEOrigins();
                for(i = 0; i < originLST.length; i++){
                    if(originLST[i].substring(1, 4) == origin) {
                        eraseOrigin = false;
                        break;
                    }
                }

                if(!eraseOrigin && destination != '' && destination != null){
                    var destinationsLST = getDestinationForIBE(origin);
                    for(i = 0; i < destinationsLST.length; i++){
                        if(destinationsLST[i].substring(1, 4) == destination) {
                            eraseDestination = false;
                            break;
                        }
                    }
                }

            }

            if(eraseOrigin) {
                $(".ibe-origin").val('');
                $("#jsIbeBookingForm .error-group-fields").attr('style', 'display:block');
                $("#jsIbeBookingForm .error-group-fields").focus();
            }

            if(eraseDestination) {
                $(".ibe-destination").val('');
                $("#jsIbeBookingForm .error-group-fields").attr('style', 'display:block');
                $("#jsIbeBookingForm .error-group-fields").focus();
            }
        }
    }

    function ValidateAdultPassengers(){

        /* ADULTS COMBOBOX CORRECTIONS - 25/7/2012 */
        var babies = $('#passenger-baby').val();
        var children = $('#passenger-child').val();
        var total = parseInt($('#passenger-adult').val()) + parseInt(children);
        var valid = true;


        // $('#passengerNumberError').remove()
        //$('.error-message').addClass('mod-vanished').attr('aria-hidden', 'false').focus();
        if(total > 9){
            // $('#passenger-adult').val(0);

            $('.error-list').append('<li class="error-item" id="AdultPassengerNumberError">' + 'Se permiten hasta 9 pasajeros en una reserva online. Los beb&#233;s no cuentan para este total.' + "</li>").focus();
            //  $('.error-message').removeClass('mod-vanished').attr('aria-hidden', 'false').focus();
            return false;
        }
        if(!(total > 9) && ($('#passenger-adult').val() < babies) ){

            $('.error-list').append('<li class="error-item" id="AdultPassengerNumberError">' + 'Cada adulto puede viajar con 4 ni&#241;os o con un ni&#241;o y un beb&#233;.' + "</li>").focus();
            // $('.error-message').removeClass('mod-vanished').attr('aria-hidden', 'false').focus();
            return false;
        }
        if(!(total > 9) && ($('#passenger-adult').val() > babies)){
            var maxChildren = parseInt(($('#passenger-adult').val()-babies)*4) + parseInt(babies);
            if(children > maxChildren){

                $('.error-list').append('<li class="error-item" id="AdultPassengerNumberError">' + 'Cada adulto puede viajar con 4 ni&#241;os o con un ni&#241;o y un beb&#233;.' + "</li>").focus();
                // $('.error-message').removeClass('mod-vanished').attr('aria-hidden', 'false').focus();
                return false;
            }
        }
        if(!(total > 9) && ($('#passenger-adult').val() == babies)){
            if(children>$('#passenger-adult').val()){

                $('.error-list').append('<li class="error-item" id="AdultPassengerNumberError">' + 'Cada adulto puede viajar con 4 ni&#241;os o con un ni&#241;o y un beb&#233;.' + "</li>").focus();
                // $('.error-message).removeClass('mod-vanished').attr('aria-hidden', 'false').focus();
                return false;
            }
        }
        /* if(error)
             $('#passenger-adult').val(lastAdultVal);
         else
             lastAdultVal = $('#passenger-adult').val();
         /* END OF CORRECTIONS */

        /*if (!IS_IE_7 && !IS_IE_8 && !IS_MOBILE_BROWSER)
			$('#passenger-child').resetSS();

		if (!IS_IE_7 && !IS_IE_8 && !IS_MOBILE_BROWSER)
			$('#passenger-baby').resetSS();
		if (!IS_IE_7 && !IS_IE_8 && !IS_MOBILE_BROWSER)
			$(this).resetSS();*/


        return true;
    }

    function ValidateBabyPassengers(){

        var valid = true;

        var adults = $('#passenger-adult').val();
        var children = $('#passenger-child').val();
        var babies = $('#passenger-baby').val();

        if( $('#passenger-baby').val() > adults ){

            $('.error-list').append('<li class="error-item" id="BabyPassengerNumberError">' + 'Cada adulto puede viajar con 4 ni&#241;os o con un ni&#241;o y un beb&#233;.' + "</li>").focus();

            return false;
        }

        if($('#passenger-baby').val() == adults){
            if(children>adults)
            {
                var max=$('#passenger-baby').val();
                while( max>-1)
                {
                    max--;
                    //alert(max);
                    if(children<=(adults - max)*4+(adults-max))
                    {

                        $('.error-list').append('<li class="error-item" id="BabyPassengerNumberError">' + 'Cada adulto puede viajar con 4 ni&#241;os o con un ni&#241;o y un beb&#233;.' + "</li>").focus();
                        // $('.error-message').removeClass('mod-vanished').attr('aria-hidden', 'false').focus();
                        return false;
                        //break;
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        if($('#passenger-baby').val() < adults){
            var maxChildren = parseInt((adults-babies)*4) + parseInt(babies);
            //var maxChildren = 100;
            if(children > maxChildren)
            {
                $('.error-list').append('<li class="error-item" id="passengerNumberError">' + 'Cada adulto puede viajar con 4 ni&#241;os o con un ni&#241;o y un beb&#233;.' + "</li>").focus();
                // $('.error-message').removeClass('mod-vanished').attr('aria-hidden', 'false').focus();
                return false;
                //$(this).val(0);
            }
        }
        /*if (!IS_IE_7 && !IS_IE_8 && !IS_MOBILE_BROWSER)
		$(this).resetSS();*/

        return true;

    }

    function ValidateChildPassengers(){

        var valid = true;

        var adults = $('#passenger-adult').val();
        var babies = $('#passenger-baby').val();
        var total = parseInt($('#passenger-child').val()) + parseInt(adults);
        if(total > 9){
            // $('#passenger-adults').val(0);
            // $('#passenger-adults').resetSS();
            //$('#passenger-child').val(0);
            $('.error-list').append('<li class="error-item" id="ChildPassengerNumberError">' + 'Se permiten hasta 9 pasajeros en una reserva online. Los beb&#233;s no cuentan para este total.' + "</li>").focus();
            // $('.error-message').removeClass('mod-vanished').attr('aria-hidden', 'false').focus();
            return false;
        }


        if(  babies <= adults ){
            var maxChildren = parseInt((adults-babies)*4) + parseInt(babies);

            if( $('#passenger-child').val() > maxChildren ){
                //$('#passenger-child').val( maxChildren );
                // $('#passenger-child').val((adults - babies)*4);
                $('.error-list').append('<li class="error-item" id="ChildPassengerNumberError">' + 'Cada adulto puede viajar con 4 ni&#241;os o con un ni&#241;o y un beb&#233;.' + "</li>").focus();
                // $('.error-message').removeClass('mod-vanished').attr('aria-hidden', 'false').focus();
                return false;
            }

        }
        if(babies==adults){

            if( $('#passenger-child').val() > adults  ){
                //$('#passenger-child').val(adults);
                //$('#passenger-child').val(adults);
                $('.error-list').append('<li class="error-item" id="ChildPassengerNumberError">' + 'Cada adulto puede viajar con 4 ni&#241;os o con un ni&#241;o y un beb&#233;.' + "</li>").focus();
                //$('.error-message').removeClass('mod-vanished').attr('aria-hidden', 'false').focus();
                return false;
            }
        }
        /*if (!IS_IE_7 && !IS_IE_8 && !IS_MOBILE_BROWSER)
			$(this).resetSS();
			*/

        return true;
    }



    function ValidatePassengers(){


        $('#AdultPassengerNumberError').remove()
        $('#ChildPassengerNumberError').remove()
        $('#BabyPassengerNumberError').remove()
        //$('.error-message').addClass('mod-vanished').attr('aria-hidden', 'false').focus();

        var validAdultPassengers = ValidateAdultPassengers();
        if(validAdultPassengers == false){

            $('.error-message').removeClass('mod-vanished').attr('aria-hidden', 'false').focus();
            return false;
        }

        var validChildPassengers = ValidateChildPassengers();

        if(validChildPassengers == false){
            $('.error-message').removeClass('mod-vanished').attr('aria-hidden', 'false').focus();

            return false;
        }
        var validBabyPassengers = ValidateBabyPassengers();
        if(validBabyPassengers == false){
            $('.error-message').removeClass('mod-vanished').attr('aria-hidden', 'false').focus();
            return false;
        }

        return true;
    }


    document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded",function () {

        /* START datepicker Range AND Single */
        $(function(){

            if($('.js-daterangepicker').length){

                $('.js-daterangepicker').each(function(index){
                    if(!$(this).hasClass('js-mobile-mode')){
                        generateRangeDatepicker(this, index);
                    }
                });
            }

            /* SINGLE DATE PICKER */
            if($('.js-datesinglepicker').length){

                $('.js-datesinglepicker').each(function(index){
                    if(!$(this).hasClass('js-mobile-mode')){
                        generateSingleDatepicker(this, index);
                    }
                });
            }
        });
        /* END datepicker Range AND Single */

        $(function() {
            $(".js-anytime").attr('href', "/es-ar/");
            $(".js-anytime").attr('title', "");
            $(".js-anytime").attr('target', "");
            $(".js-anytime").text("Cualquier fecha");

            $('.js-anytime').on('click', function(evt){
                evt.preventDefault();

                var formData = buildFormData();

                if(formData.Origin && formData.Destination){

                    var data = JSON.stringify({
                        'formData': formData,
                        'renderingId': 'f665bd7a-5b51-45f0-af88-bde2b66e5043'
                    });

                    $.ajax({
                        url: "/toolbar/anytimeBooking",
                        type: "POST",
                        data: data,
                        contentType: "application/json",
                        async: false,
                        success: function (response) {
                            if(response.Status != "200")
                            {
                                alert("Error");
                            }
                            else {
                                window.location = response.Url;
                            }
                        },
                        error: function (status) {
                            console.log("Error");
                        }
                    })
                }
            });

            var localeFormat = moment().localeData().longDateFormat('L');
            var InitialSearchDay = moment().add(1, "days").format(localeFormat);
            $("#jsIbeBookingForm23323 #date-departure").val(InitialSearchDay);
            $("#jsIbeBookingForm23323 #date-only-departure").val(InitialSearchDay);
        });

        var preference = getPreferedAirport();
        if(preference){
            var origin = $('#origin');
            origin.val(preference);
        }

        function buildFormData(){
            var formData = {"BookingToolFormID":0,"Origin":"","Destination":null,"OneWayStartDate":null,"RoundTripStartDate":null,"RoundTripEndDate":null,"AdultPassengers":0,"ChildPassengers":0,"BabyPassengers":0,"NumberOfPassengers":0,"CompanyId":null,"PromoCode":null,"AreDatesFlexible":false,"OnlyDirectFlights":false,"BookingCurrency":null,"TripType":null,"MulticityUrl":"https://book.flytap.com/r3air/tap/DeepLink.aspx?market=AR\u0026language=es\u0026searchType=multi"};
            formData.Origin = $("#origin").val();
            formData.Destination = $("#destination").val();
            if($('#booking-type-2').parent().hasClass('checked')){
                formData.BookingCurrency = "2";
            }
            else{
                formData.BookingCurrency = "1";
            }
            formData.TripType = $('input[name="journey-type"]:checked').val();

            var oneWayMoment= moment($("#date-only-departure").val(), 'L');
            if(oneWayMoment.isValid()){
                var oneWayDate = new Date(Date.UTC(oneWayMoment.year(), oneWayMoment.month(), oneWayMoment.date(), 0, 0, 1));
                formData.OneWayStartDate = oneWayDate
            }


            var departureMoment = moment($("#date-departure").val(), 'L');
            if(departureMoment.isValid()){
                var departureDate = new Date(Date.UTC(departureMoment.year(), departureMoment.month(), departureMoment.date(), 0, 0, 1));
                formData.RoundTripStartDate = departureDate
            }


            var returnMoment = moment($("#date-return").val(), 'L');
            if(returnMoment.isValid()){
                var returnDate = new Date(Date.UTC(returnMoment.year(),  returnMoment.month(),  returnMoment.date(), 0, 0, 1));
                formData.RoundTripEndDate = returnDate
            }


            formData.AdultPassengers = $("#passenger-adult").val();
            formData.ChildPassengers = $("#passenger-child").val();
            formData.BabyPassengers = $("#passenger-baby").val();

            var roundtrip = $('#journey-return').parent().hasClass('checked');
            if(roundtrip){
                formData.TripType = "roundtrip";
            }
            else{
                formData.TripType = "oneway";
            }

            formData.AreDatesFlexible = $('#detail-flexibe-dates').parent().hasClass('checked');
            formData.OnlyDirectFlights = $('#detail-flight').parent().hasClass('checked');


            return formData;
        }

        $('#multiCityLink').click(function(){
            var formDataMulti = buildFormData();
            if(formDataMulti.BookingCurrency == "2"){
                window.location = getMulticityMilesUrl(null,formDataMulti, "es", "AR")
            }
            else{
                window.location = multiCityComercial;
            }

        });

        $('#passenger-adult').change( function(){
            ValidatePassengers();
        });

        $('#passenger-child').change( function(){
            ValidatePassengers();
        });

        $('#passenger-baby').change( function(){
            ValidatePassengers();
        });

        $('#passengers-total').val('1');
        $('#passenger-adult').val('1');
        $('#passenger-child').val('0');
        $('#passenger-baby').val('0');

        $("#bookingSearchButton").click(function () {

            $("#jsIbeBookingForm .error-group-fields").attr('style', 'display:none');

            var formValid = $('#jsIbeBookingForm').valid()
            var validPassengers = ValidatePassengers();

            if (formValid == true && validPassengers == true) {

                var formData = buildFormData();
                var data = JSON.stringify({
                    'formData': formData,
                    'renderingId': 'f665bd7a-5b51-45f0-af88-bde2b66e5043'
                });
                setSearchedFlights(formData.Origin, formData.Destination);
                if(formData.BookingCurrency == "2"){
                    postBookWithMiles("", $('.tool.js-tab-content'), formData, "es", "pt");
                }
                else{
                    $.ajax({
                        url: "/toolbar/booking" + "?sc_mark=" + "AR" + "&sc_lang=" + "es-ES",
                        type: "POST",
                        data: data,
                        contentType: "application/json",
                        async: false,
                        success: function (response) {
                            if(response.Status != "200")
                            {
                                alert("Error");
                            }
                            else {

                                window.location = response.Url;
                            }
                        },
                        error: function (status) {
                            console.log("Error");
                        }
                    })
                }
            }
        });

        $('#booking-payment-drag').click(function() {

            SetBookingAutocomplete();

        });

        $('#destination').focusout(function () {
            if ($("#jsIbeBookingForm .error-group-fields").css("display") == "block") {
                $("#jsIbeBookingForm .error-group-fields").attr('style', 'display:none');
            }
        });

        $('#origin').focusout(function () {
            if ($("#jsIbeBookingForm .error-group-fields").css("display") == "block") {
                $("#jsIbeBookingForm .error-group-fields").attr('style', 'display:none');
            }
        });
    });
</script>

       <script aria-hidden="true">
    document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function () {

        $.validator.addMethod("condCheckinField", function (value, element) {
            var reservationCode = $("#reservationCode2").val();
            var loyaltyNumber = $("#LoyaltyNumber").val();

            if (reservationCode == "" && loyaltyNumber == "") {
                return false;
            }
            else {
                return true;
            }
        }, "");

        var checkinForm = $("#jsIbeCheckinForm").validate({
            onfocusout: function (element) { $(element).valid(); },
            ignore: ":hidden",
            highlight: function (element, errorClass) {
                $(element).closest('.ipt-wrapper').addClass('error-field');
                $(element).closest('.checker-wrapper').addClass('error-field');
            },
            unhighlight: function (element, errorClass) {
                $(element).closest('.ipt-wrapper').removeClass('error-field');
                $(element).closest('.checker-wrapper').removeClass('error-field');
            },
            focusInvalid: false,
            invalidHandler: function (e, validator) {
                i = 0;
                for (var i in validator.errorMap) {
                    var label = (($(".ipt-label[for='" + i + "']").clone().find('.mod-hidden').remove().end().text()) || ($(".ipt-label-block[for='" + i + "']").clone().find('.mod-hidden').remove().end().text()));
                    $('.error-list').append('<li class="error-item"><strong>' + label + ':</strong> ' + validator.errorMap[i] + "</li>").focus();
                }
            },
            errorPlacement: function (error, element) {
                error.appendTo($('[id=' + $(element).attr('id') + ']').closest('.ipt-wrapper, .checker-wrapper'));
            },
            errorClass: "text",
            rules: {
                'FormData.CheckInOrigin': {
                    required: true
                },
                'FormData.ReservationCode': {
                    condCheckinField: true,
                    maxlength: 6
                },
                'FormData.LoyaltyNumber': {
                    condCheckinField: true
                }
            }
            //messages: messages
        });

        var selectedFlightDate;

        $('#reservationDate').on('change', function () {
            selectedFlightDate = dates[this.value];
        });
        var select = document.getElementById('reservationDate');
        var dates = [];
        var date;
        for (var i = 0; i < 3; i++) {
            var opt = document.createElement('option');
            if (i == 0) {
                date = moment();
            }
            else {
                date = moment().add(i, 'days');
            }
            opt.value = i;
            opt.moment = date;
            opt.text = date.format('L');
            dates.push(date);
            select.appendChild(opt);
        }
        selectedFlightDate = dates[0];

        $("#checkintoolButton").click(function () {

            if ($('#jsIbeCheckinForm').valid()) {

                var formData = {};

                // var mili = selectedFlightDate.getTime();
                //formData.ReservationDate = selectedFlightDate.toString('YYYY-MM-DD HH:mm:ss');
                formData.ReservationDate = selectedFlightDate.format('YYYY-MM-DD HH:mm:ss');
                formData.ReservationCode = $("#reservationCode2").val();
                formData.LoyaltyNumber = $("#LoyaltyNumber").val();

                var data = JSON.stringify({
                    'formData': formData,
                    'renderingId': 'e0d590d4-4637-4e60-bd12-c47d5591f354'
                });
                $.ajax({
                    url: "/toolbar/checkin",
                    type: "POST",
                    data: data,
                    contentType: "application/json",
                    success: function (response) {
                        if (response.Result == "201") {

                        } else {
                            if (parseInt(selectedFlightDate.month()+1) < 10) {
                                month = "0" + (selectedFlightDate.month() + 1);
                            }
			    else
			    {
				month = "" + (selectedFlightDate.month() + 1);
			    }
                            data = selectedFlightDate.date() + "/" + month + "/"
                                + (selectedFlightDate.year());
                            
                            var url = response.Url.replace("{date}", data);

                            var modal = $('#checkin-confirm');
                            if (modal && modal.length > 0) {
                                $('#js-show-modal-checkin-confirm').click();
                                $("#checkin-confirm").attr('href', url);
                            }
                            else {
                                var checkinTab = window.open(url, "checkIn");
                                checkinTab.focus();
                            }
                        }
                    },
                    error: function (status) {
                        console.log("Error");
                    }
                })
            }
        });
    });
</script>

       <script>



    document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded",function () {
        var selectedFlightInfoDate;
        $('#flightInfoDate').on('change', function () {
            selectedFlightInfoDate = datesInfo[this.value];
        });
        var selectInfo = document.getElementById('flightInfoDate');
        var datesInfo = [];
        var dateInfo;
        for (var i = 0; i < 3; i++) {
            var opt = document.createElement('option');
            if (i == 0) {
                dateInfo = moment();
            }
            else {
                dateInfo = moment().add(i, 'days');
            }
            opt.value = i;
            opt.moment = dateInfo;
            opt.text = dateInfo.format('L');
            datesInfo.push(dateInfo);
            selectInfo.appendChild(opt);
        }
        selectedFlightInfoDate = datesInfo[0];

        $('#departure').on('change', function () {
            if ($('span[class="checked"][name="flightInfoRadioOption"]').find("input").val() == 1)
            {
                if($("#departure").val() == 2){
                    $("#departureAirport").attr('placeholder', "Aeropuerto de llegada");
                }
                else
                {
                    $("#departureAirport").attr('placeholder', "Aeropuerto de salida");
                }
            }
        });

        $('.ipt-wrapper.departures').on('chgPlcHolder', function() {
            if ($('span[class="checked"][name="flightInfoRadioOption"]').find("input").val() != 1)
            {
                 $("#departureAirport").attr('placeholder', "Aeropuerto de salida");
            }
            else
            {
                if($("#departure").val() == 2){
                    $("#departureAirport").attr('placeholder', "Aeropuerto de llegada");
                }
            }
        });

        //TODO Ajax Call to login User

    $("#flightInfoContinueButton").on('click', function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        if ($('#jsIbeFlightForm').valid()) {

            var formData = {"FlightDate":"\/Date(-62135596800000)\/","Date":null,"FlightNumber":null,"DepartureAiport":null,"ArrivalAirport":null,"StandaloneAirport":null,"SearchOption":null,"FlightType":null,"ReservationDateId":null,"ReservationDates":[{"Disabled":false,"Group":null,"Selected":false,"Text":"03/10/2017","Value":"1"},{"Disabled":false,"Group":null,"Selected":false,"Text":"04/10/2017","Value":"2"},{"Disabled":false,"Group":null,"Selected":false,"Text":"05/10/2017","Value":"3"}]};
            formData.FlightNumber = $("#tpNumber-toolbar").val();
            formData.FlightDate = selectedFlightInfoDate.format('YYYY-MM-DD HH:mm:ss');
            formData.StandaloneAirport = $("#StandaloneAirport").val();
            formData.DepartureAiport = $("#departureAirport").val();
            formData.ArrivalAirport = $("#arrivalAirport").val();
            formData.SearchOption = $('span[class="checked"][name="flightInfoRadioOption"]').find("input").val();
            formData.ReservationDateId =  $("#reservationDate2").val();
            formData.FlightType = $("#departure").val();

            var data = JSON.stringify({
                formData: formData,
            });

            $.ajax({
                url: "/toolbar/flightInfoTool?sc_mark=AR"+"&sc_lang=es-ES",
                type: "POST",
                data: data,
                headers: {
                    'RequestVerificationToken': $('input[name=__RequestVerificationToken]').val()
                },
                contentType: "application/json",
                success: function (status) {
                    if(status.Result == "500") {
                        $.each(status.ErrorList, function (key, val) {
                            var label = val.Field;
                            $('.error-list').append('<li class="error-item">' +'<strong>' + val.Field + ': ' +'</strong>' + val.ErrorMessage + "</li>").focus();
                        });
                        $('.error-message').removeClass('mod-vanished').attr('aria-hidden', 'false').focus();
                    } else {
                        window.location.href = status;
                    }
                },
                error: function (status) {
                    alert("Error - Ajax Post Flight Info Tool");
                }
            })
        }
    });
    });
</script>

       <script>

    document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded",function () {

        //TODO Ajax Call to login User
        $("#booking-confirm").click(function () {

            if ($('#jsIbeChangeForm').valid()) {

                $('.error-list').empty();

                var formData = {"LastName":null,"ReservationCode":null};
                formData.ReservationCode = $("#reservationCode").val();
                formData.LastName = $("#lastname").val();

                var data = JSON.stringify({
                    'formData': formData,
                    'renderingId': '6360f332-d89f-40a7-a3ff-3d60b4197eeb'
                });

                
                
                $.ajax({
                    url: "/toolbar/ChangeBooking",
                    type: "POST",
                    data: data,
                    contentType: "application/json",
                    success: function (response) {
                        if(response.Status == "500") {
                            $('.error-list').append('<li class="error-item">' + response.Message + "</li>").focus();
                            $('.error-message').removeClass('mod-vanished').attr('aria-hidden', 'false').focus();
                        } 
                        else {
                            var modal = $('#manage-booking-confirm');
                            if(modal && modal.length > 0){
                                $('#js-show-modal-booking-confirm').click();
                                $("#manage-booking-confirm").attr('href', response.Url) 
                            }
                            else{
                                var manageTab = window.open("about:blank","manage");
                                manageTab.location = response.Url;
                                manageTab.focus();
                            }
                                                       
                        }
                    },
                    error: function (status) {
                        alert("Error");
                    }
                })
            }
        });

        $("#printRecipeButton").click(function () {

            if ($('#jsIbePrintForm').valid()) {

                $('.error-list').empty();

                var formData = {"LastName":null,"TicketNumber":null};
                formData.LastName = $("#lastname2").val();
                formData.TicketNumber = $("#ticketNumber").val();

                var data = JSON.stringify({
                    'formData': formData,
                    'renderingId': '6360f332-d89f-40a7-a3ff-3d60b4197eeb'
                });

                $.ajax({
                    url: "/toolbar/printRecipe",
                    type: "POST",
                    data: data,
                    contentType: "application/json",
                    success: function (response) {
                        if(response.Status == "500") {
                            $('.error-list').append('<li class="error-item">' + response.Message + "</li>").focus();
                            $('.error-message').removeClass('mod-vanished').attr('aria-hidden', 'false').focus();
                        } else {
                            var x = window.open(response.Url, '_blank');
                            if (x) {
                                win.focus();
                            } else {
                                alert('Please allow popups for this website');
                            }
                        }
                    },
                    error: function (status) {
                        alert("Error");
                    }
                })
            }
        });


    });
</script>

        $('.js-recentSearch').on('click', function (e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            var theInput = $(this).parent().find('.js-autocomplete').trigger('focus');
            // Exeption to not trigger focus-autocomplete inputs when ibe-tools is not open
            if (theInput.hasClass('no-autocomplete')) {
                theInput.removeClass('no-autocomplete').trigger('focus');
            }
            if (window.innerWidth <= 767) {
                theInput.removeClass('no-autocomplete').trigger('click');

        var searchTags = [
        ];

        var favotitesTags = [
        ];

        var autocompleteTags;

        var lastResearch;

        // Language terms
        var lang_lastResearches = "&#218;ltimas b&#250;squedas",
            lang_showMore = "Ver m&#225;s",
            lang_delete = "Borrar",
            lang_suggestDestination = "Sugerir un destino",
            lang_seeAll = "Ver todo",
            lang_allAirports = "Ver todos los aeropuertos";

        var accentMap = {
            "ç": "c", "ý": "y", "ÿ": "y", "þ": "b", "": "f", "ñ": "n",
            "à": "a", "á": "a", "â": "a", "ã": "a", "å": "a", "ä": "a",
            "ò": "o", "ó": "o", "ô": "o", "ö": "o", "õ": "o", "ø": "o",
            "è": "e", "é": "e", "ê": "e", "ë": "e",
            "ì": "i", "í": "i", "î": "i", "ï": "i",
            "ù": "u", "ú": "u", "û": "u",
        };

        var normalize = function (term) {
            var ret = "";
            for (var i = 0; i < term.length; i++) {
                ret += accentMap[term.charAt(i)] || term.charAt(i);
            }
            return ret;
        };

        var autocompleteClicked;
        if (window.innerWidth >= 768) {
            $('.js-autocomplete').each(function (i, el) {

                var quickSearchInput = false;

                el = $(el);
                $(el).closest('.ipt-wrapper').append('<div class="autocomplete-holder"><div class="autocomplete-results"></div><div class="autocomplete-footer"><ul></ul></div></div>')
                var theInput = $(el).closest('.ipt-wrapper').find('input');
                if (theInput.attr('type') == 'search' && theInput.hasClass('ipt-sm-search')
                    || theInput.attr('type') == 'search' && theInput.hasClass('ipt-search')) {
                    //                console.log('É INPUT SEARCH DESKTOP');
                    quickSearchInput = true;
                }

                var autocompleteHolder = $(el).closest('.ipt-wrapper').find('.autocomplete-holder');
                var resultContainer = $(el).closest('.ipt-wrapper').find('.autocomplete-holder .autocomplete-results');
                var footerContainer = $(el).closest('.ipt-wrapper').find('.autocomplete-holder .autocomplete-footer > ul');
                el.autocomplete({
                    appendTo: resultContainer,
                    minLength: 0,
                    search: function (event, ui) {
                        $('.list-results ul').empty();
                        footerContainer.empty();
                    },
                    source: function (request, response) {
                        if (el.hasClass('js-airport')) {
                            autocompleteTags = airportTags;
                        } else if (el.hasClass('js-ibeairport-origin')) {
                            autocompleteTags = getIBEOrigins();
                            autocompleteTags = sortAirportFilter(autocompleteTags, request.term);
                        } else if (el.hasClass('js-ibevictoriaairport-origin')) {
                            autocompleteTags = getIBEVictoriaOrigins();
                        } else if (el.hasClass('js-ibeairport-checkin-origin')) {
                            autocompleteTags = getIBEOriginsWithOnlineCheckIn();
                        } else if (el.hasClass('js-ibeairport-destination')) {
                            var origin = $('.js-ibeairport-origin').val();
                            if (origin) {
                                autocompleteTags = getDestinationForIBE(origin.substring(1, 4));
                                autocompleteTags = sortAirportFilter(autocompleteTags, request.term);
                            }
                            else {
                                autocompleteTags = [];
                            }

                        } else if (el.hasClass('js-ibevictoriaairport-destination')){

                            var origin = $('.js-ibevictoriaairport-origin').val();
                            if (origin) {
                                autocompleteTags = getDestinationForVictoria(origin.substring(1, 4));

                            }
                            else {
                                autocompleteTags = [];
                            }
                        } else if (el.hasClass('js-city')) {
                            autocompleteTags = destinationCityTags;
                        } else if (el.hasClass('js-country')) {
                            autocompleteTags = allCountryTags;
                        } else if (el.hasClass('js-all-country')) {
                            autocompleteTags = allCountryTags;
                        } else if (el.hasClass('js-all-city')) {
                            autocompleteTags = allCityTags;
                        } else if (el.hasClass('js-all-markets')) {
                            autocompleteTags = marketTags;
                        } else {
                            autocompleteTags = searchTags;
                        }

                        var matcher = new RegExp($.ui.autocomplete.escapeRegex(request.term.toLowerCase()), "i");
                        var results = $.grep(autocompleteTags, function (value) {
                            value = value.label || value.value || value;
                            return matcher.test(value.toLowerCase()) || matcher.test(normalize(value.toLowerCase()));
                        });

                        //var results = $.ui.autocomplete.filter(autocompleteTags, request.term);
                        //response(results.slice(0, 4));
                        if (!quickSearchInput) {
                            response(results.slice(0, 4));
                        }

                    },
                    select: function (event, ui) {
                        if ($(this).valid) {
                            $(this).val(ui.item.value);
                            $(this).valid();
                        }
                        if ($(this).hasClass('js-ibeairport-origin')) {
                            $('.js-ibeairport-destination').val("");
                        }
                    },
                    open: function (event, ui) {
                        var widget = $(this).data('ui-autocomplete'),
                            menu = widget.menu,
                            $ul = menu.element,
                            id = $ul.attr('id');

                        var numElementsShow = 3;
                        var numToShow = 3;

                        var _fieldID = $(this).attr('id');

                        if ($(this).val() == '') {
                            $('#' + id + ' .ui-menu-item').hide();
                        }

                        // Recent Searches inside autocomplete
                        if ($(this).parent().find('.js-recentSearch').length) {
                            $('#' + id).append('<li class="ui-custom-menu-item ui-custom-title clock"><span class="ui-custom-stp stp-circle-theme">' + recentSearches + '</span>' + lang_lastResearches + '</li>');
                            $.each(recentsearchesTags, function (key, value) {
                                var hideStatus = '';
                                if (key > numElementsShow - 1) {
                                    hideStatus = 'mod-vanished';
                                }
                                $('#' + id).append('<li class="ui-custom-menu-item ui-custom-book-flight-link ' + hideStatus + '"><a data-index=" ' + key + ' " href="#!" class="cta"><span class="airport-code">' + value[0] + '</span><strong>' + value[1] + '</strong><span class="form-icn-plane"></span><span class="airport-code">' + value[2] + '</span><strong>' + value[3] + '</strong><span class="date">' + value[4] + '</span></a></li>');
                            });

                            /* set values on two inputs*/
                            $('.ui-custom-book-flight-link .cta').on('click', function (e) {
                                e.preventDefault();
                                var index = Number($(this).data('index'));
                                $('.js-autocomplete-fields > .ipt-wrapper:eq(0) input.ui-autocomplete-input').val(recentsearchesTags[index][0] + ' ' + recentsearchesTags[index][1]);
                                $('.js-autocomplete-fields > .ipt-wrapper:eq(1) input.ui-autocomplete-input').val(recentsearchesTags[index][2] + ' ' + recentsearchesTags[index][3]);
                                $('.js-autocomplete-fields > .ipt-wrapper:eq(0) input.ui-autocomplete-input').blur();
                                footerContainer.hide();
                                resultContainer.find("ul.ui-autocomplete").hide();
                            });

                            $('.ui-autocomplete').append('<li class="ui-custom-menu-item ui-custom-link"><a href="#">' + lang_showMore + '</a></li>');

                            /* shows three more results */
                            $('#' + id).find('.ui-custom-link').on('click', function (e) {
                                e.preventDefault();

                                for (var i = numElementsShow; i < numElementsShow + numToShow; i++) {
                                    $('#' + id).find('.ui-custom-menu-item.ui-custom-book-flight-link:eq( ' + i + ' )').removeClass('mod-vanished');
                                }
                                if (numElementsShow + numToShow > recentSearches) {
                                    $(this).hide();
                                }
                                numToShow += numToShow;
                            });

                        } else {

								$("ul.suggestion-list").empty();
								$("ul.recent-search-list").empty();
								$(".recent-search .title").remove();

								if($(this).val().length >= 1) {
									if(!$(this).parent().children('.js-deleteValue').length) {
										$(this).parent().append('<a href="#" class="stp stp-circle-delete js-deleteValue">' + lang_delete + '</a>');
									}

								} else {
									$(this).parent().children('.js-deleteValue').remove();

									$('.ui-autocomplete').each(function() {
										$(this).removeClass('virtual-modal');
									});
								}

								if ($(this).val() == '') {
									$('#' + id + ' .ui-menu-item').hide();
								}

								if ($(this).hasClass('js-destination')) {
									$('.ui-autocomplete').append('<li class="ui-custom-menu-item ui-custom-title world ui-custom-link"><a href="/es-ar/destinos/mapa-de-destinos">' + lang_suggestDestination + '</a></li>');
								}
                        }

                        // Autocomplete type
                        if ($(this).hasClass('js-place') && window.innerWidth >= 768) {
                            if (($(this).hasClass('js-airport') || $(this).hasClass('js-ibeairport-origin') || $(this).hasClass('js-ibeairport-destination')) && !$(this).hasClass('js-notAll')) {
                                $('.ui-autocomplete').append('<li id="forID-' + _fieldID + '" class="ui-custom-menu-item ui-custom-title plane ui-custom-link"><a href="#" type="button" class="js-showModal js-pickAirport" id="js-show-modal-airports">' + lang_allAirports + '</a></li>');
                            } else if (!$(this).hasClass('js-notAll')) {
                                $('.ui-autocomplete').append('<li class="ui-custom-menu-item ui-custom-title world ui-custom-link"><a href="#">' + lang_seeAll + '</a></li>');
                            }
                        }

                        // Delete input value
                        $('.js-deleteValue').click(function (e) {
                            e.preventDefault();
                            if ($(this).siblings().hasClass('js-country-expandcity')) {
                                $('.js-city-countrydependent').val('').siblings('.js-deleteValue').remove();

                                if (!($('.js-state-cloak').hasClass('mod-hidden'))) {
                                    $('#select-by-state').val('');
                                    $('.js-state-cloak').addClass('mod-hidden');
                                }
                            }
                            $(this).parent().children('.ipt').val('').focus();
                            $(this).remove();
                        });
                        /* fix when is on bottom of others results */
                        if (!$(this).val() == '') {
                            footerContainer.find('.ui-custom-menu-item').addClass('no-border-top');
                        } else {
                            footerContainer.find('.ui-custom-menu-item').removeClass('no-border-top');
                        }
                        /* Add Scroll on results - Desktop */
                        if ($('#' + id + ' .ui-menu-item').length > 5 && window.innerWidth >= 768) {
                            $('#' + id).addClass('auto-scroll');
                        }
                        footerContainer.find('.ui-custom-link:not(.showmore,.suggest) > a').on('click', function (e) {
                            e.preventDefault();
                            footerContainer.hide();
                            resultContainer.find("ul.ui-autocomplete").hide();
                        });
                        // Modal function reboot
                        $('.js-showModal,.js-hideModal').controlModal();

                    },
                    close: function (event, ui) {
                        resultContainer.find("ul.ui-autocomplete").show();
                        $(document).on('mouseup', autocompleteHolder, clickoutside);
                        function clickoutside(e) {
                            var container = autocompleteHolder;

                            if (!container.is(e.target) && container.has(e.target).length === 0) {
                                footerContainer.hide();
                                footerContainer.empty();
                                resultContainer.find("ul.ui-autocomplete").hide();
                                $(document).off('mouseup', clickoutside);
                            }
                        }
                    },
                    select: function (event, ui) {
                        var itemSelected = ui.item.value;
                        inputSelect = event.target.id;
                        footerContainer.hide();
                        resultContainer.find("ul.ui-autocomplete").hide();
                    }
                }).focus(function () {
                    // Exeption to not trigger focus-autocomplete inputs when ibe-tools is not open
                    if (!$(this).hasClass('no-autocomplete')) {
                        $('.autocomplete-holder .autocomplete-footer > ul').hide();
                        $("ul.ui-autocomplete").hide();
                        $(this).autocomplete('search');
                    }
                }).blur(function () { });
            });
        }
        else {
            $('.js-autocomplete.ui-autocomplete-input').click(function (event) {
                event.preventDefault();
                autocompleteClicked = event.target.id;
            });

            $('#back').click(function (e) {
                e.preventDefault();
                $('.ui-widget-results').hide(200);
                $('html, body, .site').removeClass('mod-scrolled-lock');
            });

            // Mobile
            $('.js-autocomplete').click(function (e) {

                var theForm = $(this).parents('.ipt-wrapper'),
                    quickSearchInput = false;

                if (theForm.find('input').attr('type') == 'search' && theForm.find('input').hasClass('ipt-sm-search')
                    || theForm.find('input').attr('type') == 'search' && theForm.find('input').hasClass('ipt-search')) {
                    //                console.log('É INPUT SEARCH MOBILE');
                    quickSearchInput = true;
                }

                if (window.innerWidth <= 767 && !$(this).hasClass('js-tagit')) {
                    /* build mobile closest-cities list */
                    var closestCitiesStatus = false;
                    if ($(this).hasClass('js-closest-cities')) {
                        closestCitiesStatus = true;
                        $("ul.closest-cities-list").empty();
                        for (var i = 0; i <= favotitesTags.length - 1; i++) {
                            var li = $('<li class="ui-menu-item" />').append(favotitesTags[i]).appendTo($('ul.closest-cities-list'));
                            li.click(function (e) {
                                var itemSelected = $(this).text();
                                var inputSelect = $('.ui-widget-results').find('input')[0].id;
                                $('input[name="' + inputSelect + '"]').val(itemSelected);
                                $('.ui-widget-results').hide(200);
                                $('html, body, .site').removeClass('mod-scrolled-lock');
                            });
                        }
                    } else {
                        $('.closest-cities').hide();
                    }
                    /* build mobile recent-search list */
                    $("ul.suggestion-list").empty();
                    $(".suggestion-list").css('display', 'none');

                    $("ul.recent-search-list").empty();
                    $(".recent-search .title").remove();
                    if ($(this).parent().find('.js-recentSearch').length) {

                        $("ul.recent-search-list").empty();
                        $(".recent-search .title").remove();

                        $('<div class="title">' + lang_lastResearches + '</div>').insertBefore("ul.recent-search-list");


                        $.each(recentsearchesTags, function (key, value) {
                            var li = $('<li class="ui-custom-menu-item ui-custom-book-flight-link"><a data-index=" ' + key + ' " href="#!" class="cta"><span class="airport-code">' + value[0] + '</span>' + value[1] + '<span class="form-icn-plane"></span><span class="airport-code">' + value[2] + '</span>' + value[3] + '<span class="date">' + value[4] + '</span></a></li>').appendTo($('ul.recent-search-list'));
                            li.click(function (e) {
                                var index = Number($(this).find('a').data('index'));

                                $('.js-autocomplete-fields > .ipt-wrapper:eq(0) input.ui-autocomplete-input').val(recentsearchesTags[index][0] + ' ' + recentsearchesTags[index][1]);
                                $('.js-autocomplete-fields > .ipt-wrapper:eq(1) input.ui-autocomplete-input').val(recentsearchesTags[index][2] + ' ' + recentsearchesTags[index][3]);

                                //var itemSelected = recentsearchesTags[index][0] + ' ' + recentsearchesTags[index][1];
                                //var inputSelect = $('.ui-widget-results').find('input')[0].id;
                                //$('input[name="' + inputSelect + '"]').val(itemSelected);
                                $('.ui-widget-results').hide(200);
                                $('html, body, .site').removeClass('mod-scrolled-lock');
                            });
                        });

                    }


                    $(".ui-widget-input").empty();
                    var theForm = $(this).parents('.ipt-wrapper');
                    if (theForm.find('input').attr('type') == 'search') {
                        var actionData = theForm.find('input').data('action');
                        theForm.clone(true).appendTo(".ui-widget-input").wrap('<form id="modal-search" action="' + actionData + '"></form>');
                    } else {
                        theForm.clone(true).appendTo(".ui-widget-input");
                    }

                    $('.ui-widget-results').show(200);
                    $('html, body, .site').addClass('mod-scrolled-lock');

                    var input = $(".ui-widget-input .ipt-mask input");
                    input.click().focus();

                    // Double the length because Opera is inconsistent about whether a carriage return is one character or two.
                    var len = input.val().length * 2;
                    if (len != 0) {
                        input[0].setSelectionRange(len, len);
                    }

                    $('.ui-widget-results .js-autocomplete').each(function (i, el) {
                        el = $(el);

                        el.autocomplete({
                            minLength: 0,
                            source: function (request, response) {

                                if (el.hasClass('js-airport')) {
                                    autocompleteTags = airportTags;
                                } else if (el.hasClass('js-ibeairport-origin')) {
                                    autocompleteTags = getIBEOrigins();
                                } else if (el.hasClass('js-ibevictoriaairport-origin')){
                                    autocompleteTags = getIBEVictoriaOrigins();
                                } else if (el.hasClass('js-ibeairport-checkin-origin')) {
                                    autocompleteTags = getIBEOriginsWithOnlineCheckIn();
                                } else if (el.hasClass('js-ibeairport-destination')) {
                                    var origin = $('.js-ibeairport-origin').val();
                                    if (origin) {
                                        autocompleteTags = getDestinationForIBE(origin.substring(1, 4));
                                    }
                                    else {
                                        autocompleteTags = [];
                                    }
                                } else if (el.hasClass('js-ibevictoriaairport-destination')){
                                    var origin = $('.js-ibevictoriaairport-origin').val();
                                    if (origin) {
                                        autocompleteTags = getDestinationForVictoria(origin.substring(1, 4));
                                    }
                                    else {
                                        autocompleteTags = [];
                                    }

                                }else if (el.hasClass('js-city')) {
                                    autocompleteTags = destinationCityTags;
                                } else if (el.hasClass('js-country')) {
                                    autocompleteTags = allCountryTags;
                                } else if (el.hasClass('js-all-country')) {
                                    autocompleteTags = allCountryTags;
                                } else if (el.hasClass('js-all-city')) {
                                    autocompleteTags = allCityTags;
                                } else if (el.hasClass('js-all-markets')) {
                                    autocompleteTags = marketTags;
                                } else {
                                    autocompleteTags = searchTags;
                                }

                                var matcher = new RegExp($.ui.autocomplete.escapeRegex(request.term.toLowerCase()), "i");
                                var results = $.grep(autocompleteTags, function (value) {
                                    value = value.label || value.value || value;
                                    return matcher.test(value.toLowerCase()) || matcher.test(normalize(value.toLowerCase()));
                                });

                                //var results = $.ui.autocomplete.filter(autocompleteTags, request.term);
                                response(results);

                            },
                            open: function (event, ui) {

                                var widget = $(this).data('ui-autocomplete'),
                                        menu = widget.menu,
                                        $ul = menu.element,
                                        id = $ul.attr('id');

                                var numElementsShow = 3;
                                var numToShow = 3;

                                var _fieldID = $(this).attr('id');

                                if ($(this).val() == '') {
                                    $('#' + id + ' .ui-menu-item').hide();
                                }

                                if ($(this).val().length >= 1) {
                                    if (!$(this).parent().children('.js-deleteValue').length) {
                                        $(this).parent().append('<a href="#" class="stp stp-circle-delete js-deleteValue">' + lang_delete + '</a>');
                                    }

                                } else {
                                    $(this).parent().children('.js-deleteValue').remove();

                                    $('.ui-autocomplete').each(function () {
                                        $(this).removeClass('virtual-modal');
                                    });
                                }


                                if ($(this).val() == '') {
                                    $('#' + id + ' .ui-menu-item').hide();
                                }

                                if ($(this).hasClass('js-destination')) {
                                    // $('.ui-autocomplete').append('<li class="ui-custom-menu-item ui-custom-title world ui-custom-link"><a href="/es-ar/destinos/mapa-de-destinos">' + lang_suggestDestination + '</a></li>');
                                }
                                // Delete input value
                                $('.js-deleteValue').click(function (e) {
                                    e.preventDefault();
                                    $(this).parent().children('.ipt').val('').focus();
                                    $(this).remove();
                                });

                                $(this).autocomplete("widget").appendTo(".list-results");
                            },
                            response: function (event, ui) {
                                if (!quickSearchInput) {
                                    if (ui.content.length === 0) {
                                        $("#empty-results").html("<p>Sin resultados</p>");
                                        if (closestCitiesStatus) {
                                            $(".closest-cities").css('display', 'block');
                                        }
                                        $(".suggestion-list").css('display', 'block');
                                    } else {
                                        if ($(this).val().length === 0) {
                                            if (closestCitiesStatus) {
                                                $(".closest-cities").css('display', 'block');
                                            }
                                            $(".suggestion-list").css('display', 'none');
                                        }
                                        else {
                                            $("#empty-results").empty();
                                            //$(".closest-cities").css('display', 'none');
                                            $(".suggestion-list").css('display', 'block');
                                        }
                                    }
                                }
                            },
                            select: function (event, ui) {
                                var itemSelected = ui.item.value;
                                inputSelect = event.target.id;
                                var inputElement = $('form #' + inputSelect + '');
                                inputElement.val(itemSelected);
                                if (inputElement.valid) {
                                    inputElement.valid();
                                }
                                $('.ui-widget-results').hide(200);
                                $('html, body, .site').removeClass('mod-scrolled-lock');
                            }

                        }).focus(function () {
                            $(this).autocomplete('search', $(this).val());
                        });
                    });
                }
            });
        }

        $.validator.addMethod("validAirport", function (value, element) {
            var found = false;
            var regex = /\(([^)]+)\)/;
            var matches = regex.exec(value);
            if (matches != null) {
                if (matches.length > 0) {
                    for (var i = 0; i < airportTags.length; i++) {
                        if (regex.exec(airportTags[i]) != null && regex.exec(airportTags[i])[1] == matches[1]) {
                            found = true;
                            break;
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            return this.optional(element) || found;
        }, "Airport not found");

        $.validator.addMethod("validIBEOriginAirport", function (value, element) {
            var ibeOrigins = getIBEOrigins();
            var found = false;
            var regex = /\(([^)]+)\)/;
            var matches = regex.exec(value);
            if (matches != null) {
                if (matches.length > 0) {
                    for (var i = 0; i < ibeOrigins.length; i++) {
                        var originCheck = regex.exec(ibeOrigins[i]);
                        if (originCheck != null && originCheck[1] == matches[1]) {
                            found = true;
                            break;
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            return this.optional(element) || found;
        }, "Airport not found");

        $.validator.addMethod("validIBEDestinationAirport", function (value, element, origin) {
            var ibeDestinations = getDestinationForIBE(origin);
            var found = false;
            var regex = /\(([^)]+)\)/;
            var matches = regex.exec(value);
            if (matches != null) {
                if (matches.length > 0) {
                    for (var i = 0; i < ibeDestinations.length; i++) {
                        if (regex.exec(ibeDestinations[i])[1] == matches[1]) {
                            found = true;
                            break;
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            return this.optional(element) || found;
        }, "Airport not found");

        $.validator.addMethod("validIBEOriginAirportVictoria", function (value, element) {
            var ibeVictoriaOrigins = getIBEVictoriaOrigins();
            var found = false;
            var regex = /\(([^)]+)\)/;
            var matches = regex.exec(value);
            if (matches != null) {
                if (matches.length > 0) {
                    for (var i = 0; i < ibeVictoriaOrigins.length; i++) {
                        if (regex.exec(ibeVictoriaOrigins[i])[1] == matches[1]) {
                            found = true;
                            break;
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            return this.optional(element) || found;
        }, "Airport not found");

        $.validator.addMethod("validIBEDestinationAirportVictoria", function (value, element, origin) {
            var ibeVictoriaDestinations = getDestinationForVictoria(origin);
            var found = false;
            var regex = /\(([^)]+)\)/;
            var matches = regex.exec(value);
            if (matches != null) {
                if (matches.length > 0) {
                    for (var i = 0; i < ibeVictoriaDestinations.length; i++) {
                        if (regex.exec(ibeVictoriaDestinations[i])[1] == matches[1]) {
                            found = true;
                            break;
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            return this.optional(element) || found;
        }, "Airport not found");

        //Validate through regex method
        $.validator.addMethod(
			"regex",
			function (value, element, regexp) {
			    var re = new RegExp(regexp[0]);
			    return this.optional(element) || re.test(value);
			},
			function (a, b) {
			    return "Formato inválido (" + a[1] + ")";
			}
		);

        //Validate if field has non alphabetic characters
        $.validator.addMethod("alphabeticRegex", function (value, element) {
            return this.optional(element) || /^[a-zA-ZÀ-ÿ^\s]+$/i.test(value);
        }, "Introduzca solo letras.");

        //Validate if field has non alpha-numeric characters
        $.validator.addMethod("nonChineseRegex", function (value, element) {
            var chineseReg = /[\u4e00-\u9fa5]+/i;
            return this.optional(element) || !(chineseReg.test(value));
        }, "Introduzca solo letras.");

        //Validate email field
        $.validator.addMethod("emailRegex", function (value, element) {
            return this.optional(element) || /^.+@.+\.([A-Za-z]{2,})$/i.test(value);
        }, "E-mail no v&#225;lido.");

        //Validate TP Number field
        $.validator.addMethod("tpNumberRegex", function (value, element) {
            return this.optional(element) || /^\d{9}$/i.test(value);
        }, "N&#250;mero Victoria no v&#225;lido.");

        //Validate email or TP Number field
        $.validator.addMethod("emailTPNumberRegex", function (value, element) {
            var tpNumb = /^[0-9]+$/i;
            if (tpNumb.test(value)) {
                if ((value.length <= 9) || (!tpNumb.test(value))) {
                    return this.optional(element) || tpNumb.test(value);
                }
            } else {
                var email = /^.+@.+\.([A-Za-z]{2,})$/i;
                if (email.test(value)) {
                    return this.optional(element) || email.test(value);
                }
            }
        }, "Datos no v&#225;lidos.");

        //Validate password field
        $.validator.addMethod("passwordRegex", function (value, element) {
            return this.optional(element) || /^[a-zA-Z0-9!@#$%_]+$/i.test(value);
        }, "Su contrase&#241;a tiene que tener al menos 8 caracteres, una letra min&#250;scula, una letra may&#250;scula y un n&#250;mero.");

        //Validate password or Pin field
        $.validator.addMethod("passwordPinRegex", function (value, element) {
            var pinNumb = /^[0-9]+$/i;
            if (pinNumb.test(value)) {
                if (((value.length >= 4) && ((value.length <= 6))) || (!pinNumb.test(value))) {
                    return this.optional(element) || pinNumb.test(value);
                }
            } else {
                var password = /^[a-zA-Z0-9!@#$%_]+$/i;
                if (((value.length <= 6)) || (password.test(value))) {
                    return this.optional(element) || password.test(value);
                }
            }
        }, "Formato de PIN no v&#225;lido. Aseg&#250;rese de haber introducido el PIN actual.");

        //Validate datepicker related fields
        $.validator.addMethod("date", function (value, element) { return true; });
        $.validator.addMethod("datepickerRegex", function (value, element) {
            return this.optional(element) || moment(value, 'L').isValid();
        }, "Introduzca una fecha v&#225;lida.");
        $.validator.addMethod('endLargerThanStart', function (value, element, param) {
            var start = moment($(param).val(), 'L');
            var end = moment(value, 'L')
            return this.optional(element) || !start.isAfter(end);
        }, "La fecha de regreso no puede ser anterior a la fecha da salida.");

        //Validate monthpicker related fields
        $.validator.addMethod("monthpickerRegex", function (value, element) {
            return this.optional(element) || /^((1[0-2]|0[1-9])\/([1-9][0-9][0-9][0-9]))$/i.test(value);
        }, "Introduzca una fecha v&#225;lida.");


        //Validate promocode field
        $.validator.addMethod("promoCodeRegex", function (value, element) {
            return this.optional(element) || /^[a-zA-Z0-9]+$/i.test(value);
        }, "C&#243;digo promocional no v&#225;lido.");

        //Validate if inputs are different - Deixei genérico porque pode ser necessário em mais campos.
        $.validator.addMethod("notEqualTo", function (value, element, param) {
            return this.optional(element) || value != $(param).val();
        }, "Los valores no pueden coincidir.");

        //Validate if the combination of first and last name does not exceed 30 characters plus 1 for space
        $.validator.addMethod("namesMaxChars", function (value, element, param) {
            return this.optional(element) || ($("#firstname").val().length + $("#lastname").val().length < 32);
        }, "La combinaci&#243;n de nombre y apellidos no puede exceder los 60 caracteres.");

        //Validate phone number
        $.validator.addMethod("phoneMaxChars", function (value, element) {
            return this.optional(element) || ($("#phoneArea").val().length + $("#phoneNumber").val().length < 20);
        }, "El n&#250;mero de tel&#233;fono no puede exceder los 19 d&#237;gitos.");

        //General messages
        $.extend($.validator.messages, {
            required: "Campo obligatorio.",
            digits: "Introduzca solo n&#250;meros.",
            email: "Introduzca un e-mail v&#225;lido.",
            date: "Introduzca una fecha v&#225;lida.",
            minlength: "Introduzca, al menos, {0} caracteres.",
            maxlength: "No introduzca m&#225;s de {0} caracteres.",
            rangelength: "Introduzca un valor entre {0} y {1} caracteres."
        });
        // CUSTOM Messages //
        var messages = {
            arrivalAirport: { notEqualTo: "Os campos de partida e destino devem ser diferentes." },
            'date-return': { notEqualTo: "As datas de partida e regresso devem ser diferentes." }
        };

        $("#jsIbeChangeForm").validate({
            onfocusout: function (element) { $(element).valid(); },
            ignore: ":hidden",
            highlight: function (element, errorClass) {
                $(element).closest('.ipt-wrapper').addClass('error-field');
                $(element).closest('.checker-wrapper').addClass('error-field');
            },
            unhighlight: function (element, errorClass) {
                $(element).closest('.ipt-wrapper').removeClass('error-field');
                $(element).closest('.checker-wrapper').removeClass('error-field');
            },
            focusInvalid: false,
            invalidHandler: function (e, validator) {
                i = 0;
                for (var i in validator.errorMap) {
                    var label = (($(".ipt-label[for='" + i + "']").clone().find('.mod-hidden').remove().end().text()) || ($(".ipt-label-block[for='" + i + "']").clone().find('.mod-hidden').remove().end().text()));
                    $('.error-list').append('<li class="error-item"><strong>' + label + ':</strong> ' + validator.errorMap[i] + "</li>").focus();
                }
            },
            errorPlacement: function (error, element) {
                error.appendTo($('[id=' + $(element).attr('id') + ']').closest('.ipt-wrapper, .checker-wrapper'));
            },
            errorClass: "text",
            rules: {
                'lastname': {
                    required: true,
                    minlength: 2,
                    alphabeticRegex: true,
                    maxlength: 30
                },
                'reservationCode': {
                    required: true,
                    minlength: 6,
                    maxlength: 6
                },
            },
            messages: messages
        });

        $("#jsIbePrintForm").validate({
            onfocusout: function (element) { $(element).valid(); },

                    $('.error-list').append('<li class="error-item"><strong>' + label + ':</strong> ' + validator.errorMap[i] + "</li>").focus();

            },
            errorPlacement: function (error, element) {

            errorClass: "text",

        $("#jsIbeCancelForm").validate({
            onfocusout: function (element) { $(element).valid(); },
            ignore: ":hidden",
            highlight: function (element, errorClass) {
                $(element).closest('.ipt-wrapper').addClass('error-field');
                $(element).closest('.checker-wrapper').addClass('error-field');
            },
            unhighlight: function (element, errorClass) {
                $(element).closest('.ipt-wrapper').removeClass('error-field');
                $(element).closest('.checker-wrapper').removeClass('error-field');
            },
            focusInvalid: false,
            invalidHandler: function (e, validator) {

        $("#jsIbeFlightForm").validate({

                    $('.error-list').append('<li class="error-item"><strong>' + label + ':</strong> ' + validator.errorMap[i] + "</li>").focus();
