        var form = $("#jsIbeBookingForm").validate({

            onfocusout: function (element) {
                /* only validate if there's no datepicker open & no dropper visible*/
                if(!$(element).hasClass('active')
                && !$('.datepicker-wrapper > .js-datepicker.hasDatepicker').length
                && !$('.datepicker-wrapper > .js-datepicker3.hasDatepicker').length
                && !$('.datepicker-wrapper > .js-datepicker4.hasDatepicker').length
                && !$('.datepicker-wrapper > .js-datepicker5.hasDatepicker').length
                && !$('.datepicker-wrapper > .js-datepicker6.hasDatepicker').length
                && !$('.datepicker-wrapper > .js-datepicker7.hasDatepicker').length
                && $('.ipt-dropper.js-noBlur').css('display') == 'none'
                && element.id != "destination" && element.id != "origin"
                   ) { $(element).valid(); }
            },
            ignore: ":hidden",
            highlight: function (element, errorClass) {
                $(element).closest('.ipt-wrapper').addClass('error-field');
                $(element).closest('.checker-wrapper').addClass('error-field');
            },
            unhighlight: function (element, errorClass) {
                $(element).closest('.ipt-wrapper').removeClass('error-field');
                $(element).closest('.checker-wrapper').removeClass('error-field');
            },
            focusInvalid: false,
            invalidHandler: function (e, validator) {
                i = 0;
                for (var i in validator.errorMap) {
                    var label = (($(".ipt-label[for='" + i + "']").clone().find('.mod-hidden').remove().end().text()) || ($(".ipt-label-block[for='" + i + "']").clone().find('.mod-hidden').remove().end().text()));
                    $('.error-list').append('<li class="error-item"><strong>' + label + ':</strong> ' + validator.errorMap[i] + "</li>").focus();
                }
            },
            errorPlacement: function (error, element) {
                error.appendTo($('[id=' + $(element).attr('id') + ']').closest('.ipt-wrapper, .checker-wrapper'));
            },
            errorClass: "text",
            rules: {
                'origin': {
                    required: true
                },
                'destination': {
                    required: true
                },

                'date-only-departure': {
                    required: true,
                    nonChineseRegex: true,
                    datepickerRegex: true,
                    maxlength: 10
                },
                'date-departure': {
                    required: true,
                    nonChineseRegex: true,
                    datepickerRegex: true,
                    maxlength: 10
                },
                'date-return': {
                    //notEqualTo: '#date-departure',
                    endLargerThanStart: '#date-departure',
                    required: true
                },
                'passengers-total': {
                    required: true,
                    min: 1
                }
            },
            messages: messages

        });


        //Submit IBE multiple forms
        $(".js-ibe-form-sbmt").click(function () {
            $('.error-list').empty();
            var validForm = $(this.form).valid();
            var validPassengers = true;
            if ($(this.form).attr('id') == 'jsIbeBookingForm') {
                validPassengers = ValidatePassengers();
            }


            if (validForm == true && validPassengers == true) {

                $('.panel.ibe-tools.is-open').find('.error-message').addClass('mod-vanished').attr('aria-hidden', 'true');
            } else {
                $('.panel.ibe-tools.is-open').find('.error-message').removeClass('mod-vanished').attr('aria-hidden', 'false').focus();
            }
            return false;
        });
    });

        <script aria-hidden="true">
                        document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded",function () {
                            $('#reactivate-account-submit').click(function () {

                                var _thisWrapper = $("#suspended-text-box");
                                addLockingLoader(_thisWrapper);

                                var email = "";
                                var password = "";
                                var rememberMe = false;

                                if ($("#login-user-account-loginRegister").val() != "" && $("#login-pass-account-loginRegister").val() != "") {
                                    email = $("#login-user-account-loginRegister").val();
                                    password = $("#login-pass-account-loginRegister").val();
                                    if ($("#login-save-account-modal").prop("checked")) {
                                        rememberMe = true;
                                    }
                                }
                                else if ($("#login-user-account").val() != "" && $("#login-pass-account").val() != "") {
                                    email = $("#login-user-account").val();
                                    password = $("#login-pass-account").val();
                                    if ($("#login-save-account").prop("checked")) {
                                        formModel.FormData.Remember = true;
                                    }
                                }
                                //If email && password are not null reactivate users account.
                                if (email && password) {
                                    var data = {
                                        'email': email,
                                        'password': password,
                                        'remember': rememberMe
                                    };
                                    $.ajax({
                                        url: "/api/ReactivateStatusAccount",
                                        type: "POST",
                                        data: JSON.stringify(data),
                                        contentType: "application/json",
                                        success: function (response) {
                                            if (response.Status == "200") {
                                                window.location.href = response.TargetUrl;
                                            } else {
                                                removeLockingLoader(_thisWrapper);
                                            }
                                        },
                                        error: function (status) {
                                            removeLockingLoader(_thisWrapper);
                                            console.log("Error");
                                        }
                                    })
                                } else {
                                    removeLockingLoader(_thisWrapper);
                                    $('#modal-suspended').removeClass('mod-shown').attr('aria-hidden', 'false').focus();
                                }
                            });

                            $('#reactivation-cancel,#reactivation-close-btn').click(function () {
                                $('#modal-suspended').removeClass('mod-shown').attr('aria-hidden', 'false').focus();
                            });
                        });
                        </script> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <div class="modal-close-button">

   <!-- Forgot Password Modal END --> 
   <script aria-hidden="true">
        document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded",function () {

            $('#recover-password,#recover-passwordtp').keypress(function (e) {
                if (e.which == 13) {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    $("#recover-client-password-submit").trigger("click");
                }
            });
            
            $("#close-recover-pass-modal").click(function() {
                $('.error-list-modal2').empty();
                $('.error-message-modal2').addClass('mod-vanished').attr('aria-hidden', 'true');
                $('#recover-client-password-success-panel').attr('aria-hidden', 'true').hide();
                $('#recover-client-password-main-panel-1').removeClass('mod-vanished').attr('aria-hidden', 'false');
                $('input#recover-password').val('');
                $('input#recover-passwordtp').val('');
                $('.tpnumber-request').addClass('mod-vanished');
                $('#recover-client-password-main-panel-1 .js-modal-title').focusWithoutScrolling();
            });

            $('#modal-forgot-password').on('click', function(e){                    
                $('#recover-client-password-success-panel').attr('aria-hidden', 'true').hide();
                $('#recover-client-password-main-panel-1').removeClass('mod-vanished').attr('aria-hidden', 'false');
                $('input#recover-password').val('');
                $('#recover-client-password-main-panel-1 .js-modal-title').focusWithoutScrolling();
            });
            //lock click only on parent
            $('#modal-forgot-password .modal-box').on('click', function(e){                    
                e.stopPropagation();
            });


            $("#recover-client-password-submit").click(function () {
                if($("#js-recover-client-password").valid()){
                    var _thisWrapper = $("#forgot-pass-loader-div");
                    addLockingLoader(_thisWrapper);

                    var label = "Correo electrónico:";
                    var errorMessage = "Introduzca un e-mail válido.";
                    var data = {
                        "email": $("#recover-password").val(),
                        "label": label,
                        "error": errorMessage,
                        "clientNumber": $("#recover-passwordtp").val()
                    };
                    $.ajax({
                        url: "/modal/recoverpass",
                        type: "POST",
                        data: JSON.stringify(data),
                        contentType: "application/json",
                        success: function (status) {
                            if (status.Result == '200') {
                                if ($('#js-recover-client-password').valid()) {
                                    $('.error-message-modal2').addClass('mod-vanished').attr('aria-hidden', 'true');
                                    $('#recover-client-password-main-panel-1').addClass('mod-vanished').attr('aria-hidden', 'true');
                                    $('#recover-client-password-success-panel').attr('aria-hidden', 'false').show();
                                    $('#recover-client-password-success-panel .js-modal-title').focusWithoutScrolling();
                                    removeLockingLoader(_thisWrapper);
                                }
                            }
                            else if (status.Result == '401') 
                            {
                                $.each(status.ErrorList, function (key, val) {
                                    var label = val.Field;
                                    $('.ipt-label-modal.error-field').empty();
                                    $('.ipt-label-modal.error-field').append('<span class="error-item">' + val.ErrorMessage + "</span>").focus();
                                });
                                // Show TP Number for entry
                                $('.tpnumber-request').removeClass('mod-vanished');
                                removeLockingLoader(_thisWrapper);                       
                            } 
                            else 
                            {
                                $('.error-list-modal2').empty();
                                $('#input-email').addClass('error-field');
                                $('#input-emailtp').addClass('error-field');
                                $.each(status.ErrorList, function (key, val) {
                                    var label = val.Field;
                                    $('.error-list-modal2').append('<li class="error-item">' + '<strong>' + val.Field + ': ' + '</strong>' + val.ErrorMessage + "</li>").focus();
                                });
                                $('.error-message-modal2').removeClass('mod-vanished').attr('aria-hidden', 'false').focus();
                                removeLockingLoader(_thisWrapper);
                            }
                        },
                        error: function (status) {
                            removeLockingLoader(_thisWrapper);
                        }
                    })
                }
            });

            // Validator //
            $("#js-recover-client-password").validate({
                onfocusout: function (element) { 
                    var recover = $.trim($("#recover-password").val());
                    $("#recover-password").val(recover);
                    $(element).valid(); 
                },
                ignore: ":hidden",
                highlight: function (element, errorClass) {
                    $(element).closest('.ipt-wrapper-modal').addClass('error-field');
                    setTimeout(function () {
                        $(element).parent().next('.' + errorClass).css('display', 'block');
                    }, 100);
                },
                unhighlight: function (element, errorClass) {
                    $(element).closest('.ipt-wrapper-modal').removeClass('error-field');
                    setTimeout(function () {
                        $(element).parent().next('.' + errorClass).css('display', 'none');
                    }, 100);
                },
                focusInvalid: false,
                invalidHandler: function (e, validator) {
                    i = 0;
                    $('.error-list-modal2').empty();
                    for (var i in validator.errorMap) {
                        var label = (($(".ipt-label-modal[for='" + i + "']").clone().find('.mod-hidden').remove().end().text()) || ($(".ipt-label-modal-block[for='" + i + "']").clone().find('.mod-hidden').remove().end().text()));
                        $('.error-list-modal2').append('<li class="error-item"><strong>' + label + ':</strong> ' + validator.errorMap[i] + "</li>").focus();
                    }
                    $('.error-message-modal2').removeClass('mod-vanished').attr('aria-hidden', 'false').focus();
                },
                errorPlacement: function (error, element) {
                    error.appendTo($('input[id=' + $(element).attr('id') + ']').closest('.ipt-wrapper-modal'));
                },
                errorElement: "span",
                errorClass: "text",
                rules: {
                    'Email': {
                        required: true,
                        nonChineseRegex: true,
                        emailRegex: true,
                        maxlength: 200
                    },
                }
            });
        });
    </script>

   <script aria-hidden="true">
    document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded",function () {
        $('#btnFacebookModal').click(function () {
            socialfb.loginUser(function (response, data) {
                if (response.Status == "OK") {
                    location.href = "/";
                }
                else if (response.Status == "NOK") {
                    $('#button-register-redirect').click();
                }
            });
        });
    });
    </script> 
   <script aria-hidden="true">
  var googleUser = {};

  function attachSignin(element) {

    auth2.attachClickHandler(element, {},
        function (googleUser) {
            socialgoogle.validateUser(googleUser, function (data) {
                var postData = {
                    provider: 'google',
                    user_id: data.userId,
                    token: data.accessToken,
                    pictureUrl: data.imageUrl
                };
                $('#LoginFormData_AccessToken').val(data.accessToken);
                $('#LoginFormData_SocialId').val(data.userId);
                $('#LoginFormData_Provider').val('google');
                $.ajax({
                    url: "/api/SocialLogin",
                    type: "POST",
                    data: JSON.stringify(postData),
                    contentType: "application/json",
                    success: function (response) {
                        if (response.Status == "OK") {
                            location.href = "/";
                        }
                        else if (response.Status == "NOK") {
                            $('#button-register-redirect').click();
                        }
                    },
                    error: function () {

                    }
                });
            });
        }, function(error){
            alert(JSON.stringify(error, undefined, 2));
        });
  }
    </script>

   <!-- Modal Login And Register END --> 
   <script aria-hidden="true">
    document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function () {
        // CUSTOM Messages //
        var messages = {
            'login-user-account-loginRegister': {
                emailTPNumberRegex: 'Por favor, insira um email válido.'
            },
            'login-pass-account-loginRegister': {
                passwordPinRegex: 'Por favor, insira um pin válido.'
            }
        };

        $("#loginRegister-modal-submit").click(function () {

            if ($("#js-login-account-modal").valid()) {

                $('.error-message-LoginRegister').addClass('mod-vanished').attr('aria-hidden', 'true');

                var rememberMe = false;
                if($("#login-save-account-modal").prop("checked")) {
                    rememberMe = true;
                }

                var data = JSON.stringify({
                    'username': $("#login-user-account-loginRegister").val(),
                    'password': $("#login-pass-account-loginRegister").val(),
                    'remember': rememberMe
                });

                var _thisWrapper = $("#modal-login-register .modal-content");
                addLockingLoader(_thisWrapper);

                $.ajax({
                    url: "/api/LoginAjax?sc_mark=AR&sc_lang=es-ES",
                    type: "POST",
                    data: data,
                    contentType: "application/json",
                    success: function (status) {

                        if (status.Result == "201") {
                            removeLockingLoader(_thisWrapper);
                            showModal('modal-suspended');
                        } else if(status.Result == "500" || status.Result == "401") {
                            removeLockingLoader(_thisWrapper);
                            $.each(status.ErrorList, function (key, val) {
                                var label = val.Field;
                                $('.error-list-LoginRegister').append('<li class="error-item">' + '<strong>' + val.Field + ': ' + '</strong>' + val.ErrorMessage + "</li>").focus();
                            });
                            $('.error-message-LoginRegister').removeClass('mod-vanished').attr('aria-hidden', 'false').focus();
                        } else if(status.Status == "200") {
                            window.location.href = status.TargetUrl;
                        }
                        else if(status.Status == "201") {
                            removeLockingLoader(_thisWrapper);
                            if ($("modal-login-register").hasClass("mod-shown")) {
                                $("#modal-login-register").find(".modal-close-button button").trigger("click");
                            }
                            showModal('modal-suspended');
                        } else if(status.Status == "500" || status.Status == "401") {
                            removeLockingLoader(_thisWrapper);
                            $('.error-list-LoginRegister').append('<li class="error-item">' + status.Message + "</li>").focus();
                            $('.error-message-LoginRegister').removeClass('mod-vanished').attr('aria-hidden', 'false').focus();
                        } else {
                            window.location.href = status;
                        }
                    },
                    error: function (status) {
                        removeLockingLoader(_thisWrapper);
                        console.log("Error login modal");
                    }

                })

            }

        });

        // Validator //
        // GENERIC FORM VALIDATION - ADD NEW FIELDS HERE!
        $("#js-login-account-modal").validate({
            onfocusout: function (element) { $(element).valid(); },
            ignore: ":hidden",
            highlight: function (element, errorClass) {
                $(element).closest('.ipt-wrapper').addClass('error-field');
            },
            unhighlight: function (element, errorClass) {
                $(element).closest('.ipt-wrapper').removeClass('error-field');
            },
            focusInvalid: false,
            invalidHandler: function (e, validator) {
                i = 0;
                $('.error-list-login-modal').empty();
                for (var i in validator.errorMap) {
                    var label = (($(".ipt-label[for='" + i + "']").clone().find('.mod-hidden').remove().end().text()) || ($(".ipt-label-block[for='" + i + "']").clone().find('.mod-hidden').remove().end().text()));
                    $('.error-list-LoginRegister').append('<li class="error-item"><strong>' + label + ':</strong> ' + validator.errorMap[i] + "</li>").focus();
                }
            },
            errorPlacement: function (error, element) {
                error.appendTo($('[id=' + $(element).attr('id') + ']').closest('.ipt-wrapper, .checker-wrapper'));
            },
            errorClass: "text",
            rules: {
                'login-user-account-loginRegister': {
                    required: true,
                    nonChineseRegex: true,
                    emailTPNumberRegex: true,
                    maxlength: 200
                },
                'login-pass-account-loginRegister': {
                    required: true,
                    minlength: 4
                }
            },
            messages: messages
        });

        //Submit generic form
        $("#loginRegister-modal-submit").click(function () {
            $('.error-list-LoginRegister').empty();
            if ($('#js-login-account-modal').valid()) {
                $('.error-message-LoginRegister').addClass('mod-vanished').attr('aria-hidden', 'true');
            } else {
                $('.error-message-LoginRegister').removeClass('mod-vanished').attr('aria-hidden', 'false').focus();
            }
            return false;
        });

        //Hide actual modal (before show next)
        $("#js-show-modal-forgot-password").click(function () {
            $("#modal-airports .js-hideModal").click();
        });
    });
    </script> 
  </div>

Al utilizar este sitio, consiente su uso.' + '</span><span class="button"><button type=button id="warning_EU_close" class="btn btn-txt-light" title="Botão para omitir o aviso"><span class="txt"><span class="mask">Lo he entendido.</span></span></button></span></div></div>';
